<script>
    $(document).ready(function(){
        var timeout;

		$('.block-suggester-container').on('click',function(e){

			e.stopPropagation();

        });

        $('.block-suggester-container .suggester input[type=text]').keyup(function(){
            var self = $(this);

            if(timeout) clearTimeout(timeout);

            timeout = setTimeout(function(){
                $.nette.ajax({
                    url: "https:\/\/www.kosik.cz\/vitejte?do=suggester-suggest",
                    data: {
                        phrase: self.val()
                    }
                })
            }, 300);


        });

    });

    function gaPush(self, cat)
    {
        dataLayer.push({
            'event': 'ga.pageview',
            'pagePath': '/hledat?q='+$('#frm-suggester-suggester-phrase').val()+'&cat='+cat,
            'pageTitle': 'Našeptávač'
        });

        window.location = self.href;
    }
</script>

</form>

    </div>

    var ShoppingList = {
        toggle: function () {
            basic.toggleClass(document.getElementById('shopping-list-overlay'), 'active')
        }
    };

    basic.documentReady(function () {

        var textArea = document.getElementById('frm-shoppingList-listForm-queries');

        if (textArea)
            textArea.setAttribute('placeholder', 'Například: \n\nMléko \nChléb \nVejce \nMaso \nRajče \n\n\nPro zadání klikněte do pole')
    });

</script>

        <script>
            $(document).ready(function () {
                $('.region-navigation ul > li.sub').hover(function () {
                    var isOpen = $(this).data().open;

                    if (!isOpen) {
                        var images = $(this).find('img');

                        images.each(function (index, element) {
                            $(element).attr('src', $(element).data().src);
                        });

                        $(this).data().open = true;
                    }
                });
            });
        </script>

		$(document).ready(function () {

			var isOpen = $('body').hasClass('show');
			var open = 2;
			var close = 3;
			var closeDrivers=8;
			var openDrivers=6;

			$('.block-guarantee').slick({
				dots: false,
				infinite: true,
				slidesToShow: 1,
				//autoplay: true,
				//autoplaySpeed: 5000,
			});

			$('.region-facebook-posts-inner').slick({
				dots: false,
				infinite: true,
				slidesToShow: isOpen ? open : close,
				slidesToScroll: 2,
				responsive: [
					{
						breakpoint: 990,
						settings: {
							slidesToShow: 2,
							slidesToScroll: 2
						}
					},
					{
						breakpoint: 767,
						settings: {
							slidesToShow: 1,
							slidesToScroll: 1
						}
					}
				]

			});

			$('.region-drivers-carousel-inner').slick({
				dots: false,
				infinite: true,
				slidesToShow: isOpen ? openDrivers : closeDrivers,
				slidesToScroll: 2,
				responsive: [
					{
						breakpoint: 1100,
						settings: {
							slidesToShow: 7,
							slidesToScroll: 2
						}
					},
					{
						breakpoint: 991,
						settings: {
							slidesToShow: 5,
							slidesToScroll: 2
						}
					}
				]

			});

			/*$('.region-drivers-carousel-inner .landing-col').click(function () {
				$('.region-drivers-carousel-inner .landing-col.info').hide();
				var nextItem = $(this).next();
				nextItem.hide();
				nextItem.toggle("slide");
			});*/


			fixing.onClose(function () {
				$('.region-facebook-posts-inner').slick('slickSetOption', 'slidesToShow', close,  true);
				$('.region-drivers-carousel-inner').slick('slickSetOption', 'slidesToShow', closeDrivers, true);
				$('.block-guarantee').slick('slickSetOption', 'slidesToShow', 1, true);
			});

			fixing.onOpen(function () {
				$('.region-facebook-posts-inner').slick('slickSetOption', 'slidesToShow', open, true);
				$('.region-drivers-carousel-inner').slick('slickSetOption', 'slidesToShow', openDrivers, true);
				$('.block-guarantee').slick('slickSetOption', 'slidesToShow', 1, true);
			});

		});


	</script>
